<tr>
<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>The splendid <i>5th Concerto</i> of Beethoven is too difficult for any but finished artists, but this exquisite fragment from the slow movement as transcribed by Moszkowski makes a charming solo number. Grade 5.
</td></tr>
